</span><span class="x1lliihq"><ol class="x13faqbe xeaf4i8 x1n2onr6 x3yw8vx x1gslohp x12nagc xqsn43r" dir="ltr"><li dir="auto" value="1" class="x4tra6z"><span class="_ao3e _aupe copyable-text" data-testid="selectable-text" data-pre-plain-text="1. ">Core Philosophy – Compression–Release Principle</span></li>
</ol></span><span class="x1lliihq">1.1 Ground Floor = Compression
</span><span class="x1lliihq">Horizontal, grounded, and visually heavier
</span><span class="x1lliihq">Should read as calm, solid, and stable
</span><span class="x1lliihq">1.2 Upper Duplex (First + Second Floor) = Release

<ol class="x13faqbe xeaf4i8 x1n2onr6 x3yw8vx xqsn43r" dir="ltr"><li dir="auto" value="1" class="x4tra6z"><span class="_ao3e">Core Philosophy – Compression–Release Principle</span></li>
</ol>1.1 Ground Floor = Compression
Horizontal, grounded, and visually heavier
Should read as calm, solid, and stable
1.2 Upper Duplex (First + Second Floor) = Release
Lighter, taller-feeling, and more open
Should convey a clear sense of openness and vertical lift
<ol class="x13faqbe xeaf4i8 x1n2onr6 x3yw8vx xqsn43r" dir="ltr"><li dir="auto" value="2" class="x4tra6z"><span class="_ao3e">Controlled Vertical Spine – South-East Corner</span></li>
</ol>2.1 Only one restrained vertical element on the SE side,- Should start quietly near the ground floor (name-board zone)to at the end of pergola / crown level
